Sound insulation:
1. There is a big error between the endoscope of the cat's eye in the door and the diameter of the hole. When trying to turn the cover of the cat's eye, it cannot be opened, but the cat's eye turns with the finger.
2. The door and the door frame look like a perfect fit from the outside, but when viewed from inside the room, there is a relatively large gap between the door and the door frame. It is especially obvious when viewed at night. The lights in the corridor pass through the door gap. Come through.
(The above two points result in poor sound insulation, especially when guests return to their rooms at night, especially if the door is not closed)
health:
1. Perhaps because of moisture, bacteria are about to grow on the surface of the two leather containers placed on the bathroom sink, making them look dirty.
2. There is also a long mirror on the left hand side of the entrance. There is a lot of dirt on the mirror, which is very uncomfortable.
(Please clean it up quickly, guests don‚Äôt want to live in a "******* house")
equipment:
1. The air conditioner makes too much noise. It roars as soon as it is turned on. It is useless to turn down the fan speed. There is not much difference between turning it on and off. It does not heat or cool at all. Now in November, I adjust the air conditioner temperature to 25 degrees. Half an hour later, the room temperature is still 20 degrees.
2. The composite floor in front of the balcony door is hollow when you step on it, so you are worried about accidents.
3. The light control buttons are really hard to use, especially the "please disturb me" button, which can be turned on or off.
Public Safety:
1. I saw hotel employees looking at their mobile phones while riding balance bikes, especially around corners. Who knows what will happen in the next second!
2. It is best to prepare several signs with "The floor is slippery, watch your step" in the restaurant to avoid unnecessary trouble.
The above points are what I want to say to Howard Johnson
